namespace = ehof_map_stars

# on_press_begin
country_event = {
	id = ehof_map_stars.000
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ehof_versioned } }
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = ehof_versioned
		event_target:global_event_country = { set_variable = { which = ehof_version value = @ehof_version } }
	}
}

# on_monthly_pulse_country
event = {
	id = ehof_map_stars.001
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { event_target:global_event_country = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = ehof_version value = @ehof_version } } } }
	immediate = {
		event_target:global_event_country = {
			set_variable = { which = ehof_version value = @ehof_version }
			country_event = { id = ehof_map_stars.002 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ehof_map_stars.002
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {

		############### FIX COMPOUND EXPANSION
		if = {
			limit = { exists = event_target:compound_invasion_entry }
			every_system = {
				limit = {
					distance = {
						source = event_target:compound_invasion_entry
						min_jumps = 1
						max_jumps = 6
					}
					OR = {
						NOT = { exists = owner }
						AND = {
							exists = owner
							owner = { NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:compound_country } }
						}
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_star_flag = ehof_compound_system } remove_star_flag = ehof_compound_system }
				if = { limit = { has_star_flag = compound_fleet_enroute } remove_star_flag = compound_fleet_enroute }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_star_flag = compound_expand } } set_star_flag = compound_expand }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_star_flag = compound_next_target } } set_star_flag = compound_next_target }
			}
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = { is_country_type = default }

			############### FIX MEGASTRUCTURE FLAGS
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_megastructure = { has_megastructure_flag = ehof_phase_01 } }
				random_system_within_border = {
					limit = { any_system_megastructure = { has_megastructure_flag = ehof_phase_01 } }
					set_star_flag = ehof_megastructure_system@prev
					every_system_planet = { set_planet_flag = cant_build_here }
				}
				set_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 1 }
				set_country_flag = ehof_restored_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p0_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p1_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p2_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p3_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p4_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p5_first_time
				country_event = { id = ehof_megastructure.201 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_megastructure = { has_megastructure_flag = ehof_phase_02 } }
				random_system_within_border = {
					limit = { any_system_megastructure = { has_megastructure_flag = ehof_phase_02 } }
					set_star_flag = ehof_megastructure_system@prev
					every_system_planet = { set_planet_flag = cant_build_here }
				}
				set_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 }

				remove_country_flag = ehof_p3_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p4_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p5_first_time

			}
			if = {

				random_system_within_border = {
					limit = { any_system_megastructure = { has_megastructure_flag = ehof_phase_03 } }
					set_star_flag = ehof_megastructure_system@prev
					every_system_planet = { set_planet_flag = cant_build_here }
				}
				set_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 }
				set_country_flag = ehof_restored_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p0_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p1_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p2_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p3_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p4_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p5_first_time
				country_event = { id = ehof_megastructure.201 }

				}

				set_country_flag = ehof_restored_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p0_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p1_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p2_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p3_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p4_first_time
				remove_country_flag = ehof_p5_first_time
				country_event = { id = ehof_megastructure.201 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_megastructure = { has_megastructure_flag = ehof_phase_05 } }
				random_system_within_border = {
					limit = { any_system_megastructure = { has_megastructure_flag = ehof_phase_05 } }
					set_star_flag = ehof_megastructure_system@prev
					every_system_planet = { set_planet_flag = cant_build_here }
				}
				set_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 5 }
				set_country_flag = ehof_restored_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p0_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p1_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p2_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p3_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p4_first_time
				set_country_flag = ehof_p5_first_time
				country_event = { id = ehof_megastructure.201 }
			}

			############### FIX REALITY CODE
			# Code 2 missing
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ehof_code_1_complete
					NOR = {
						any_planet_within_border = {
							exists = archaeological_site
							archaeological_site = {
								is_site_type = code2_digsite
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = ehof_code_2_complete
					}
				}
				random_system_within_border = {
					limit = {
						ehof_cohesive_system = yes
						any_system_planet = {
							is_colony = no
							is_asteroid = no
							is_star = no
							has_anomaly = no
							NOT = { exists = archaeological_site }
						}
					}
					random_system_planet = {
						limit = {
							is_colony = no
							is_asteroid = no
							is_star = no
							has_anomaly = no
							NOT = { exists = archaeological_site }
						}
						change_pc = pc_broken
						add_anomaly = { category = code_2_cat }
						set_planet_flag = code_world2@event_target:ehof_system_creator
					}
				}
			}
			# Code 3 missing
			if = {
				limit = {

						any_system_planet = {
							is_colony = no
							is_asteroid = no
							is_star = no

							is_colony = no
							is_asteroid = no
							is_star = no
							has_anomaly = no
							NOT = { exists = archaeological_site }
						}
						change_pc = pc_frozen
						add_anomaly = { category = code_3_cat }
						set_planet_flag = code_world3@event_target:ehof_system_creator
					}
				}
			}
			# Code 4 missing
			if = {

					star = {
						add_anomaly = { category = code_6_cat }
						set_planet_flag = code_world6@event_target:ehof_system_creator
					}
				}
			}

			############### FIX SENTIENT METAL
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ehof_code_1_complete
					NOR = {
						has_failed_special_project = SELF_REPLICATING_ALLOYS
						has_completed_special_project = SELF_REPLICATING_ALLOYS
						is_researching_special_project = SELF_REPLICATING_ALLOYS
						has_special_project = SELF_REPLICATING_ALLOYS
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = extracted_sentient_metal
				random_system_within_border = {
					limit = {
						any_system_megastructure = {
							OR = {
								is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway_disabled
								is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway_unknown
								is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway_restored
								is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway
							}
						}
					}
					random_system_ambient_object = {
						limit = { has_ambient_object_flag = fake_pylon }
						enable_special_project = {
							name = "SELF_REPLICATING_ALLOYS"
							owner = root
							location = this
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		############### FIX PYLONS
		every_system = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_megastructure = ehof_gateway
					has_megastructure = ehof_gateway_restored
					has_megastructure = ehof_gateway_disabled
					has_megastructure = ehof_gateway_unknown
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_megastructure = ehof_gateway
						has_megastructure = ehof_gateway_restored
					}
					NOT = { any_system_ambient_object = { has_ambient_object_flag = fake_pylon } }
				}
				random_system_megastructure = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway
							is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway_restored
						}
					}
					create_ambient_object = { type = fake_pylon location = this }
					last_created_ambient_object = { set_ambient_object_flag = fake_pylon }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_megastructure = ehof_gateway_disabled
						has_megastructure = ehof_gateway_unknown
					}
					NOT = { any_system_ambient_object = { has_ambient_object_flag = fake_pylon } }
				}
				random_system_megastructure = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway_disabled
							is_megastructure_type = ehof_gateway_unknown
						}
					}
					create_ambient_object = { type = fake_stone location = this }
					last_created_ambient_object = { set_ambient_object_flag = fake_pylon }
				}
			}
		}

		############### FIX SYSTEMS
		clear_global_event_target = s_c05_01_001
		clear_global_event_target = s_c05_01_002

# On press begin
country_event = {
	id = ehof_map_stars.003
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_ai = no
			is_country_type = global_event
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_system = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_star_flag = ehof_listed } }
			set_star_flag = ehof_listed

			# Stellar Remnants (75)
			if = {
				limit = { ehof_category_05 = yes }
				set_star_flag = ehof_category_05
				random_country = {
					limit = { is_country_type = global_event }
					change_variable = { which = mapping_stellar_remnants value = 1 }
				}

				# Black Holes: 40
				if = {
					limit = { OR = { is_star_class_sc_black_hole = yes is_star_class_sc_ehof_black_hole = yes } }
					event_target:global_event_country = { change_variable = { which = mapping_sc_black_hole value = 1 } }
					set_global_flag = c05_01_exists
					if = {		limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c05_01_001 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c05_01_001 }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c05_01_002 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c05_01_002 }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c05_01_003 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c05_01_003 }

					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c05_01_010 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c05_01_010 }
